href="/profile/adityagoel28">adityagoel28</a></div><div><a href="/profile/rinakawamura">rinakawamura</a></div><div><a href="/profile/c3cili4">c3cili4</a></div><div><a href="/profile/ayen2">ayen2</a></div><div><a href="/profile/Sbaessler">Sbaessler</a></div><div><a href="/profile/B0Jack">B0Jack</a></div><div><a href="/profile/nadjatee1996">nadjatee1996</a></div><div><a href="/profile/z0xd">z0xd</a></div><div><a href="/profile/lmart">lmart</a></div><div><a href="/profile/nebuchadnezzar">nebuchadnezzar</a></div><div><a href="/profile/djohn364">djohn364</a></div><div><a href="/profile/bjone314">bjone314</a></div><div><a href="/profile/NateSoul">NateSoul</a></div><div><a href="/profile/FragmentedCurve">FragmentedCurve</a></div><div><a href="/profile/rvalter">rvalter</a></div><div><a href="/profile/kgresha7">kgresha7</a></div><div><a href="/users/with/All/by/user_lastactivity/DESC/page-1">more</a></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n\t\t<div id="page">\n\n\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Inferno</div><div class="box_c"><p>For the people not familiar with challenge sites, a challenge site is mainly a site focussed on offering computer-related problems. Users can register at such a site and start solving challenges. There exist lots of different challenge types. The most common ones are the following: <b>Cryptographic, Crackit, Steganography, Programming, Logic and Math/Science</b>. The difficulty of these challenges vary as well.</p><p>When I first started out I was familiar with working with a computer, but that was about it. In about 5 years I roamed the internet searching for different kind of challenge sites. I have played at many different sites, did a lot of challenges and I am still learning new (and exciting) stuff.</p><p>I also found an IRC network where most of the bigger challenge sites have their own IRC channel. These channels often have bots allowing users to check how other people are ranked at a certain site, or sites. From time to time the screens are filled with these simple requests. That is the reason I started coding this site. It allows the users to get a complete overview of a users challenge history on every site he signed up for. Now how does this work exactly?</p><p>A user on this site can indicate which challenge sites he plays at with a specific username. Challenge sites can be selected from a simple drop-down list. His profile page will then contain an entry for this specific challenge site with the given username, along with some text describing how high he is ranked at that site. This will give a complete overview of one user in an instance.</p><p>Please forgive me if the list is not complete. There are lots of challenge sites out there and probably lots of them I do not know about. I will try to give a complete list of challenge sites to choose from, and I will also provide a piece of code for challenge site owners so that their site can be listed on this site as well.</p><p>Kind regards,<br/><br/>Inferno</p></div></div>\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Gizmore</div><div class="box_c"><p>The goal is to make a global ranking for challengers.</p><p>Also we like to give an overview of popular challenge sites, and encourage challengers to try them out.</p><p>Beside that, WeChall is my coding playground :)</p></div></div>\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Kender</div><div class="box_c"><p>Well, I had this server in a datacenter that was not doing much.. :)</p><p>And just like a lot of people, I had thoughts about creating a cross-challenge-site statistics site.</p><p>I hope that we can get more people to enjoy playing challenge sites, and provide a starting point to discover other sites than the ones you already play.</p></div></div>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<div id="page_footer_space"></div>\n\t</div>\n\t<footer id="gwf_footer"><nav id="gwf_foot_menu">\n<a href="/news">News</a>\n| <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3/commits/master">Changes</a>\n| <a href="/about_wechall">About Us</a>\n| <a href="/join_us">Join Us</a>\n| <a href="/links">Links</a>\n| <a href="/active_sites">Sites</a>\n| <a href="/forum">Forum</a>\n| <a href="/ranking">Ranking</a>\n| <a href="/challs">Challenges</a>\n| <a href="/irc_chat">Chat</a>\n| <a href="/contact">Contact</a>\n</nav>\n<div id="foot_boxes" class="cf">\n<div class="foot_box">\xc2\xa92008-2021 by wechall.net; Challenges will be added/updated regularly. Anyone from the community can contribute challenges, please reach out by email or discord.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nSo, who are the3000?<br />\r\n<blockquote class="gwf_bb_quote"><div class="gwf_bb_quote_top"><span>Quote from rekter0</span></div>A collection of students, hobbyists and professionals deeply interested in Cyber Security playing CTFs and doing info-sec research.<br />\r\nWe are committed to deliver an interesting and most of all a fun learning experience.</blockquote><br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-86-New_Site_PWN_TN-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_85">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Aug 14, 2020 - 11:46</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/gizmore">gizmore</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>PromptRiddle joined</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Dear Challengers,<br />\r\n<br />\r\nI am happy to announce that a new site has joined the wechall network.<br />\r\n<br />\r\n<a href="https://promptriddle.com/">PromptRiddle</a> is from Brazil and it seems to be in english.<br />\r\nI did not check out the site much, but the name is clever. It even has a prompt theme and soundtrack.<br />\r\nThe challenge categories shall be Crypto, Stegano and Logic whereas 57 challenges are available.<br />\r\nIn the beginning it really looks more like a puzzle/riddle side, not that techy so far... but this seems to change later on.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe authors want to add this in the news:<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe game has a hackish-theme and is based on a computer terminal emulator.<br />\r\nThe player is in constant communication with Cyber, the fictional main<br />\r\ncharacter of Promptriddle. The passwords are usually encrypted in physical<br />\r\nresources, like in images, in texts and/or in audios. Promptriddle is still<br />\r\ngrowing and has currently 57 levels online. Each level may be independent<br />\r\nor not from the previous ones.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nIn the name of Daniel Bentes Ferreira, Eduardo Dadalto C\xc3\xa2mara Gomes and Leonardo Cesar Wolter<br />\r\n<br />\r\nwe all wish you...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br />\r\n<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-85-PromptRiddle_joined-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_84">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Jun 12, 2020 - 22:35</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/tehron">tehron</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: PyD\xc3\xa9fis</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Another site from France just joined the WeChall network. I also<br />\r\nfound that often times people would unintentionally (or intentionally)<br />\r\nbreak a challenge either during or after solving it. I also don\'t enjoy<br />\r\nenumeration during a CTF, I prefer a straight forward problem to which you<br />\r\nneed to solve. As a solution to these frustrations, I created 247CTF which<br />\r\nis a CTF platform that does not have an end date, nor does it have<br />\r\nchallenge sharing between different players (each challenge instance is<br />\r\nunique per user), nor is significant enumeration required.<br />\r\n</blockquote><br />\r\n<br />\r\nI set a basescore of 10000 and we all wish you a <br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-81-247CTF_joined-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_80">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Aug 05, 2019 - 15:34</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/dloser">dloser</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: \xc3\x89nigmes \xc3\x80 Th\xc3\xa9matiques</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Time to learn French if you don\'t know it already: a new site has joined. mysql, sqlite, mssql, mongodb, ... and there are also some web application firewalls to keep you entertained.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe currently 49 challenges are in english and the overall site seems slim and fast.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe author <a href="/profile/rubiya">rubiya</a> created the site to make developers more aware of SQL injections, but i assume he does also like exploits.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nWe wanna welcome the Lords with a...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-79-LordofSQLi_joined-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_78">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Oct 19, 2018 - 00:00</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/gizmore">gizmore</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: MysteryTwister</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">This time we are really happy to announce...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nthat experts in the field of cryptography have joined the wechall network.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe new challenge site joining is <a href="https://www.mysterytwisterc3.org">MysteryTwister</a>, which is part of the famous open-source project CrypTool, known amongst challengers.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nCrypTool is an academic approach to teach the mathematics behind cryptography in an experimental manner by offering three offline e-learning programs (CT1, CT2, and JCT), the website CrypTool-Online, and the MysteryTwister crypto contest.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe puzzles on MTC3 are, of course, of cryptographic nature, and quite some of the problems are yet unsolved.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nMTC3 has almost 9000 players from all around the world and the ciphertexts are presented in English and German. There is an active forum to discuss the problems in a non-spoiling, moderated manner.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nCurrently there are 260 challenges by more than 50 different authors, offering everything about crypto and computational number theory I can imagine -- from classical ciphers (Caesar, Vigen\xc3\xa8re, Hill, ...) to modern symmetric and asymmetric crypto (ORYX, AES, RSA, ECC, Lattice, homomorphic, DSA, ...).<br />\r\n<br />\r\nSo if you need a warmup or a fresh excourse in cryptography, this surely is a place to look at.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe site is scheduled with 10,000 basepoints, and the wechall score also includes old and inactive challenge sets.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe project lead Bernhard Esslinger is looking forward to your feedback and,maybe, a yet unsolved challenge to be cracked.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nWe all hope that many of you discover something new while trying out the<br />\r\nsite and we wish you...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br />\r\n<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-78-New_Site_MysteryTwister-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_77">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Jul 21, 2018 - 11:42</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/dloser">dloser</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: CanHackMe</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Safflower (a.k.a. href="/profile/rinakawamura">rinakawamura</a></div><div><a href="/profile/evanv03">evanv03</a></div><div><a href="/profile/adityagoel28">adityagoel28</a></div><div><a href="/profile/c3cili4">c3cili4</a></div><div><a href="/profile/ayen2">ayen2</a></div><div><a href="/profile/Sbaessler">Sbaessler</a></div><div><a href="/profile/B0Jack">B0Jack</a></div><div><a href="/profile/nadjatee1996">nadjatee1996</a></div><div><a href="/profile/z0xd">z0xd</a></div><div><a href="/profile/lmart">lmart</a></div><div><a href="/profile/nebuchadnezzar">nebuchadnezzar</a></div><div><a href="/profile/djohn364">djohn364</a></div><div><a href="/profile/bjone314">bjone314</a></div><div><a href="/profile/NateSoul">NateSoul</a></div><div><a href="/profile/FragmentedCurve">FragmentedCurve</a></div><div><a href="/profile/rvalter">rvalter</a></div><div><a href="/profile/kgresha7">kgresha7</a></div><div><a href="/users/with/All/by/user_lastactivity/DESC/page-1">more</a></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n\t\t<div id="page">\n\n\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Inferno</div><div class="box_c"><p>For the people not familiar with challenge sites, a challenge site is mainly a site focussed on offering computer-related problems. Users can register at such a site and start solving challenges. There exist lots of different challenge types. The most common ones are the following: <b>Cryptographic, Crackit, Steganography, Programming, Logic and Math/Science</b>. The difficulty of these challenges vary as well.</p><p>When I first started out I was familiar with working with a computer, but that was about it. In about 5 years I roamed the internet searching for different kind of challenge sites. I have played at many different sites, did a lot of challenges and I am still learning new (and exciting) stuff.</p><p>I also found an IRC network where most of the bigger challenge sites have their own IRC channel. These channels often have bots allowing users to check how other people are ranked at a certain site, or sites. From time to time the screens are filled with these simple requests. That is the reason I started coding this site. It allows the users to get a complete overview of a users challenge history on every site he signed up for. Now how does this work exactly?</p><p>A user on this site can indicate which challenge sites he plays at with a specific username. Challenge sites can be selected from a simple drop-down list. His profile page will then contain an entry for this specific challenge site with the given username, along with some text describing how high he is ranked at that site. This will give a complete overview of one user in an instance.</p><p>Please forgive me if the list is not complete. There are lots of challenge sites out there and probably lots of them I do not know about. I will try to give a complete list of challenge sites to choose from, and I will also provide a piece of code for challenge site owners so that their site can be listed on this site as well.</p><p>Kind regards,<br/><br/>Inferno</p></div></div>\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Gizmore</div><div class="box_c"><p>The goal is to make a global ranking for challengers.</p><p>Also we like to give an overview of popular challenge sites, and encourage challengers to try them out.</p><p>Beside that, WeChall is my coding playground :)</p></div></div>\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Kender</div><div class="box_c"><p>Well, I had this server in a datacenter that was not doing much.. :)</p><p>And just like a lot of people, I had thoughts about creating a cross-challenge-site statistics site.</p><p>I hope that we can get more people to enjoy playing challenge sites, and provide a starting point to discover other sites than the ones you already play.</p></div></div>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<div id="page_footer_space"></div>\n\t</div>\n\t<footer id="gwf_footer"><nav id="gwf_foot_menu">\n<a href="/news">News</a>\n| <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3/commits/master">Changes</a>\n| <a href="/about_wechall">About Us</a>\n| <a href="/join_us">Join Us</a>\n| <a href="/links">Links</a>\n| <a href="/active_sites">Sites</a>\n| <a href="/forum">Forum</a>\n| <a href="/ranking">Ranking</a>\n| <a href="/challs">Challenges</a>\n| <a href="/irc_chat">Chat</a>\n| <a href="/contact">Contact</a>\n</nav>\n<div id="foot_boxes" class="cf">\n<div class="foot_box">\xc2\xa92008-2021 by wechall.net; mysql, sqlite, mssql, mongodb, ... and there are also some web application firewalls to keep you entertained.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe currently 49 challenges are in english and the overall site seems slim and fast.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe author <a href="/profile/rubiya">rubiya</a> created the site to make developers more aware of SQL injections, but i assume he does also like exploits.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nWe wanna welcome the Lords with a...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-79-LordofSQLi_joined-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_78">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Oct 19, 2018 - 00:00</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/gizmore">gizmore</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: MysteryTwister</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">This time we are really happy to announce...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nthat experts in the field of cryptography have joined the wechall network.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe new challenge site joining is <a href="https://www.mysterytwisterc3.org">MysteryTwister</a>, which is part of the famous open-source project CrypTool, known amongst challengers.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nCrypTool is an academic approach to teach the mathematics behind cryptography in an experimental manner by offering three offline e-learning programs (CT1, CT2, and JCT), the website CrypTool-Online, and the MysteryTwister crypto contest.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe puzzles on MTC3 are, of course, of cryptographic nature, and quite some of the problems are yet unsolved.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nMTC3 has almost 9000 players from all around the world and the ciphertexts are presented in English and German. There is an active forum to discuss the problems in a non-spoiling, moderated manner.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nCurrently there are 260 challenges by more than 50 different authors, offering everything about crypto and computational number theory I can imagine -- from classical ciphers (Caesar, Vigen\xc3\xa8re, Hill, ...) to modern symmetric and asymmetric crypto (ORYX, AES, RSA, ECC, Lattice, homomorphic, DSA, ...).<br />\r\n<br />\r\nSo if you need a warmup or a fresh excourse in cryptography, this surely is a place to look at.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe site is scheduled with 10,000 basepoints, and the wechall score also includes old and inactive challenge sets.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe project lead Bernhard Esslinger is looking forward to your feedback and,maybe, a yet unsolved challenge to be cracked.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nWe all hope that many of you discover something new while trying out the<br />\r\nsite and we wish you...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br />\r\n<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-78-New_Site_MysteryTwister-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_77">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Jul 21, 2018 - 11:42</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/dloser">dloser</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: CanHackMe</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Safflower (a.k.a. St4rburst), one of our avid users, has created a new challenge site called <a href="https://canhack.me/">CanHackMe</a>. Why don\'t you go and check it out, you lazy bum? ;)<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Summer Challenging...<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-77-New_Site_CanHackMe-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n\t\n<div class="gwf_pagemenu">\n<span>\n\t<a class="gwf_pagemenu_sel" >1</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-2">2</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-3">3</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-4">4</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-5">5</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-6">6</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-7">7</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-8">8</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-9">9</a>\n\n</span>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<div class="cb"></div>\n\n\n<div class="cb"></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<div id="page_footer_space"></div>\n\t</div>\n\t<footer id="gwf_footer"><nav id="gwf_foot_menu">\n<a href="/news">News</a>\n| <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3/commits/master">Changes</a>\n| <a href="/about_wechall">About Us</a>\n| <a href="/join_us">Join Us</a>\n| <a href="/links">Links</a>\n| <a href="/active_sites">Sites</a>\n| <a href="/forum">Forum</a>\n| <a href="/ranking">Ranking</a>\n| <a href="/challs">Challenges</a>\n| <a href="/irc_chat">Chat</a>\n| <a href="/contact">Contact</a>\n</nav>\n<div id="foot_boxes" class="cf">\n<div class="foot_box">\xc2\xa92008-2021 by wechall.net; <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3">All code</a> runs under the terms of the <a href="/wechall_license">WeChall Public License</a>; You can <a href="/contact">contact us here</a>.</div>\n<div class="foot_box">77 users were online at Jan 24, 2021 - 23:32:34<br/>1398633078 pages have been served until now</div>\n<div class="foot_box"><div>59 Queries (6 writes) in 0.0140s - PHP Time: 0.0078s - Total Time: 0.0218s. href="/profile/kasyoka">kasyoka</a></div><div><a href="/profile/evanv03">evanv03</a></div><div><a href="/profile/adityagoel28">adityagoel28</a></div><div><a href="/profile/c3cili4">c3cili4</a></div><div><a href="/profile/ayen2">ayen2</a></div><div><a href="/profile/Sbaessler">Sbaessler</a></div><div><a href="/profile/B0Jack">B0Jack</a></div><div><a href="/profile/nadjatee1996">nadjatee1996</a></div><div><a href="/profile/z0xd">z0xd</a></div><div><a href="/profile/lmart">lmart</a></div><div><a href="/profile/nebuchadnezzar">nebuchadnezzar</a></div><div><a href="/profile/djohn364">djohn364</a></div><div><a href="/profile/bjone314">bjone314</a></div><div><a href="/profile/NateSoul">NateSoul</a></div><div><a href="/profile/FragmentedCurve">FragmentedCurve</a></div><div><a href="/profile/rvalter">rvalter</a></div><div><a href="/profile/kgresha7">kgresha7</a></div><div><a href="/users/with/All/by/user_lastactivity/DESC/page-1">more</a></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n\t\t<div id="page">\n\n\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Inferno</div><div class="box_c"><p>For the people not familiar with challenge sites, a challenge site is mainly a site focussed on offering computer-related problems. Users can register at such a site and start solving challenges. There exist lots of different challenge types. The most common ones are the following: <b>Cryptographic, Crackit, Steganography, Programming, Logic and Math/Science</b>. The difficulty of these challenges vary as well.</p><p>When I first started out I was familiar with working with a computer, but that was about it. In about 5 years I roamed the internet searching for different kind of challenge sites. I have played at many different sites, did a lot of challenges and I am still learning new (and exciting) stuff.</p><p>I also found an IRC network where most of the bigger challenge sites have their own IRC channel. These channels often have bots allowing users to check how other people are ranked at a certain site, or sites. From time to time the screens are filled with these simple requests. That is the reason I started coding this site. It allows the users to get a complete overview of a users challenge history on every site he signed up for. Now how does this work exactly?</p><p>A user on this site can indicate which challenge sites he plays at with a specific username. Challenge sites can be selected from a simple drop-down list. His profile page will then contain an entry for this specific challenge site with the given username, along with some text describing how high he is ranked at that site. This will give a complete overview of one user in an instance.</p><p>Please forgive me if the list is not complete. There are lots of challenge sites out there and probably lots of them I do not know about. I will try to give a complete list of challenge sites to choose from, and I will also provide a piece of code for challenge site owners so that their site can be listed on this site as well.</p><p>Kind regards,<br/><br/>Inferno</p></div></div>\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Gizmore</div><div class="box_c"><p>The goal is to make a global ranking for challengers.</p><p>Also we like to give an overview of popular challenge sites, and encourage challengers to try them out.</p><p>Beside that, WeChall is my coding playground :)</p></div></div>\n<div class="box"><div class="box_t">Kender</div><div class="box_c"><p>Well, I had this server in a datacenter that was not doing much.. :)</p><p>And just like a lot of people, I had thoughts about creating a cross-challenge-site statistics site.</p><p>I hope that we can get more people to enjoy playing challenge sites, and provide a starting point to discover other sites than the ones you already play.</p></div></div>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<div id="page_footer_space"></div>\n\t</div>\n\t<footer id="gwf_footer"><nav id="gwf_foot_menu">\n<a href="/news">News</a>\n| <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3/commits/master">Changes</a>\n| <a href="/about_wechall">About Us</a>\n| <a href="/join_us">Join Us</a>\n| <a href="/links">Links</a>\n| <a href="/active_sites">Sites</a>\n| <a href="/forum">Forum</a>\n| <a href="/ranking">Ranking</a>\n| <a href="/challs">Challenges</a>\n| <a href="/irc_chat">Chat</a>\n| <a href="/contact">Contact</a>\n</nav>\n<div id="foot_boxes" class="cf">\n<div class="foot_box">\xc2\xa92008-2021 by wechall.net; The passwords are usually encrypted in physical<br />\r\nresources, like in images, in texts and/or in audios. Promptriddle is still<br />\r\ngrowing and has currently 57 levels online. The site specializes on cryptography challenges and currently offers 80 challenges, which are a good start for anyone interested in cryptography.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-82-New_Site_CryptoHack-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_81">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Oct 03, 2019 - 12:27</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/gizmore">gizmore</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>247CTF joined</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">We are happy to announce...<br />\r\nAnother site has been put into the wechall rankings.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe site is <a href="https://247ctf.com/">https://247ctf.com/</a> which is brand new and makes a solid impression.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe author told us the following.<br />\r\n<br />\r\n<blockquote class="gwf_bb_quote"><div class="gwf_bb_quote_top"><span>Quote from &quot;two47CTF&quot;</span></div><br />\r\nI enjoy playing CTF challenges, but often found that I was not available in<br />\r\nthe short time period that the CTF was open (usually a weekend). I also<br />\r\nfound that often times people would unintentionally (or intentionally)<br />\r\nbreak a challenge either during or after solving it. I also don\'t enjoy<br />\r\nenumeration during a CTF, I prefer a straight forward problem to which you<br />\r\nneed to solve. As a solution to these frustrations, I created 247CTF which<br />\r\nis a CTF platform that does not have an end date, nor does it have<br />\r\nchallenge sharing between different players (each challenge instance is<br />\r\nunique per user), nor is significant enumeration required.<br />\r\n</blockquote><br />\r\n<br />\r\nI set a basescore of 10000 and we all wish you a <br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-81-247CTF_joined-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_80">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Aug 05, 2019 - 15:34</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/dloser">dloser</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: \xc3\x89nigmes \xc3\x80 Th\xc3\xa9matiques</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Time to learn French if you don\'t know it already: a new site has joined. It\'s called \xc3\x89nigmes \xc3\x80 Th\xc3\xa9matiques and has challenges in many topics. Get your vin, baguette and other stereotypes and throw them away because you don\'t have time for that nonsense with this many new challenges.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nBonne \xc3\x89nigmer!(?)<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-80-New_Site_nigmes_Th_matiques-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_79">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">May 28, 2019 - 19:11</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/gizmore">gizmore</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>LordofSQLi joined</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">We are happy to announce...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nA new site has joined and is scored now.<br />\r\n<br />\r\n<a href="https://los.rubiya.kr">LordofSQLi</a> is a new site from South Korea, created in summer 2018 and is focused on SQL injection.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe database systems to exploit vary; mysql, sqlite, mssql, mongodb, ... and there are also some web application firewalls to keep you entertained.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe currently 49 challenges are in english and the overall site seems slim and fast.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe author <a href="/profile/rubiya">rubiya</a> created the site to make developers more aware of SQL injections, but i assume he does also like exploits.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nWe wanna welcome the Lords with a...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-79-LordofSQLi_joined-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_78">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Oct 19, 2018 - 00:00</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/gizmore">gizmore</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: MysteryTwister</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">This time we are really happy to announce...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nthat experts in the field of cryptography have joined the wechall network.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe new challenge site joining is <a href="https://www.mysterytwisterc3.org">MysteryTwister</a>, which is part of the famous open-source project CrypTool, known amongst challengers.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nCrypTool is an academic approach to teach the mathematics behind cryptography in an experimental manner by offering three offline e-learning programs (CT1, CT2, and JCT), the website CrypTool-Online, and the MysteryTwister crypto contest.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe puzzles on MTC3 are, of course, of cryptographic nature, and quite some of the problems are yet unsolved.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nMTC3 has almost 9000 players from all around the world and the ciphertexts are presented in English and German. There is an active forum to discuss the problems in a non-spoiling, moderated manner.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nCurrently there are 260 challenges by more than 50 different authors, offering everything about crypto and computational number theory I can imagine -- from classical ciphers (Caesar, Vigen\xc3\xa8re, Hill, ...) to modern symmetric and asymmetric crypto (ORYX, AES, RSA, ECC, Lattice, homomorphic, DSA, ...).<br />\r\n<br />\r\nSo if you need a warmup or a fresh excourse in cryptography, this surely is a place to look at.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe site is scheduled with 10,000 basepoints, and the wechall score also includes old and inactive challenge sets.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nThe project lead Bernhard Esslinger is looking forward to your feedback and,maybe, a yet unsolved challenge to be cracked.<br />\r\n<br />\r\nWe all hope that many of you discover something new while trying out the<br />\r\nsite and we wish you...<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Challenging!<br />\r\n<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-78-New_Site_MysteryTwister-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n<div class="gwf_newsbox_item" id="newsid_77">\n\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_title">\n\t\t<div class="fr">\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_date">Jul 21, 2018 - 11:42</div>\n\t\t\t<div class="gwf_newsbox_author"><a href="/profile/dloser">dloser</a></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<h3>New Site: CanHackMe</h3>\n\t\t<div class="cb"></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t\t\n\t<article class="gwf_newsbox_message">Safflower (a.k.a. St4rburst), one of our avid users, has created a new challenge site called <a href="https://canhack.me/">CanHackMe</a>. Why don\'t you go and check it out, you lazy bum? ;)<br />\r\n<br />\r\nHappy Summer Challenging...<br/><br/><a href="/news-comments-77-New_Site_CanHackMe-page-1.html">0 comments ...</a></article>\n\t\n\t\t\n</div>\n\t\n<div class="gwf_pagemenu">\n<span>\n\t<a class="gwf_pagemenu_sel" >1</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-2">2</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-3">3</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-4">4</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-5">5</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-6">6</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-7">7</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-8">8</a>\n\t<a  href="/news/en/0/All+Categories/page-9">9</a>\n\n</span>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<div class="cb"></div>\n\n\n<div class="cb"></div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t\t<div id="page_footer_space"></div>\n\t</div>\n\t<footer id="gwf_footer"><nav id="gwf_foot_menu">\n<a href="/news">News</a>\n| <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3/commits/master">Changes</a>\n| <a href="/about_wechall">About Us</a>\n| <a href="/join_us">Join Us</a>\n| <a href="/links">Links</a>\n| <a href="/active_sites">Sites</a>\n| <a href="/forum">Forum</a>\n| <a href="/ranking">Ranking</a>\n| <a href="/challs">Challenges</a>\n| <a href="/irc_chat">Chat</a>\n| <a href="/contact">Contact</a>\n</nav>\n<div id="foot_boxes" class="cf">\n<div class="foot_box">\xc2\xa92008-2021 by wechall.net; <a href="https://github.com/gizmore/gwf3">All code</a> runs under the terms of the <a href="/wechall_license">WeChall Public License</a>; You can <a href="/contact">contact us here</a>.</div>\n<div class="foot_box">77 users were online at Jan 24, 2021 - 23:32:34<br/>1398633106 pages have been served until now</div>\n<div class="foot_box"><div>60 Queries (5 writes) in 0.0183s - PHP Time: 0.0106s - Total Time: 0.0289s.
